(Sequences are not valid melds).\r\n\r\nCanasta is a card game of the rummy family of games believed to be a variant of 500 Rum. Although many variations exist for two, three, five or six players, it is most commonly played by four in two partnerships with two standard decks of cards. Players attempt to make melds of seven cards of the same rank and \"go out\" by playing all cards in their hand.\r\n\r\nCanasta for two players is the same as four-handed Canasta, in a two player game, each player plays for himself.\r\n\r\nCanasta uses two complete decks of 52 playing cards (French Deck) plus the four Jokers. The dealer shuffles the pack, the player to the dealer's right cuts, and the dealer deals out 2 hands of 11 cards to each player.The remaining cards are left in a stack in the center of the table.\r\n\r\nThe player to the dealer's left has the first turn, and play then proceeds clockwise. A turn begins either by drawing the first card from the stock into the player's hand or by picking up the entire discard pile.
